    [Model] nvarchar(max) NOT NULL,

    [Year] int NOT NULL,
    [VIN] nvarchar(max) NOT NULL,
    [LicensePlate] nvarchar(max) NOT NULL,
    [EngineType] nvarchar(max) NOT NULL,
    [EngineDisplacement] int NOT NULL,
    [HorsePower] int NOT NULL,
    [Torque] int NULL,
    [Transmission] nvarchar(max) NOT NULL,
    [Gears] int NULL,
    [ExteriorColor] nvarchar(max) NOT NULL,
    [InteriorColor] nvarchar(max) NOT NULL,
    [InteriorMaterial] nvarchar(max) NOT NULL,
    [Mileage] int NOT NULL,
    [FuelType] nvarchar(max) NOT NULL,
    [FuelConsumption] float NULL,
    [BodyStyle] nvarchar(max) NOT NULL,
    [OwnersCount] int NOT NULL,
    [HasOriginalDocuments] bit NOT NULL,
    [Condition] nvarchar(max) NOT NULL,
    [IsAsiCertified] bit NOT NULL,
    [CertificationDate] datetime2 NULL,
    [IsRoadLegal] bit NOT NULL,
    [LastInspectionDate] datetime2 NULL,
    [Description] nvarchar(max) NOT NULL,
    [Price] decimal(18,2) NOT NULL,
    [CarStatus] nvarchar(max) NOT NULL,
    [CreatedAt] datetime2 NOT NULL,
    [UpdatedAt] datetime2 NOT NULL,
    [PublishedAt] datetime2 NULL,
    [IsVisible] bit NOT NULL,
    [ShipmentId] uniqueidentifier NOT NULL,
    [OrderId] uniqueidentifier NOT NULL,
    CONSTRAINT [PK_Cars] PRIMARY KEY ([CarId]),
    CONSTRAINT [FK_Cars_Orders_OrderId] FOREIGN KEY ([OrderId]) REFERENCES [Orders] ([OrderId]) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    CONSTRAINT [FK_Cars_Shipments_ShipmentId] FOREIGN KEY ([ShipmentId]) REFERENCES [Shipments] ([ShipmentId]) ON DELETE CASCADE
